# big-code-kafka-bug-001: Kafka Producer Buffer Pool Reuse Race Condition

## Task

Investigate a bug in the Apache Kafka producer where a race condition in the `BufferPool` memory management causes messages to silently appear on the wrong topic. Trace the execution path from the producer's `send()` method through batch accumulation, buffer allocation, and network transmission to identify how buffer reuse can corrupt in-flight produce requests.

## Context

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/kafka--be816b82 (mirror of apache/kafka) (Java, ~800K LOC)
- **Category**: Bug Investigation
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Entry Point**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java` — `sendProducerData()` and `failBatch()` methods

## Symptom

Users of the Kafka producer with non-zero `linger.ms` observe that messages published to topic A occasionally appear on topic B instead. The corruption is rare but occurs in bursts, typically during broker restarts or network disruptions. The CRC checksum on the records passes because it covers only key/value/headers, not the topic name. The produce request header (containing topic/partition) is serialized separately from the message payload.

The bug is a race condition: when an in-flight `ProducerBatch` expires or its broker disconnects, the batch's pooled `ByteBuffer` is returned to the `BufferPool` and immediately reused by a new batch — while the original batch's request is still being written to the network by the `Sender` thread.

## Requirements

1. Starting from the entry point, trace the execution path to the root cause
2. Identify the specific file(s) and line(s) where the bug originates
3. Explain WHY the bug occurs (not just WHERE) — focus on the buffer lifecycle
4. Propose a fix with specific code changes

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```
## Files Examined
- path/to/file1.ext — examined for [reason]
- path/to/file2.ext — examined for [reason]
...

## Dependency Chain
1. Symptom observed in: path/to/symptom.ext
2. Called from: path/to/caller.ext (function name)
3. Bug triggered by: path/to/buggy.ext (function name, line ~N)
...

## Root Cause
- **File**: path/to/root_cause.ext
- **Function**: function_name()
- **Line**: ~N
- **Explanation**: [Why this code is buggy]

## Proposed Fix
```diff
- buggy code
+ fixed code
```

## Analysis
[Detailed trace from symptom to root cause, explaining each step]
```

## Evaluation Criteria

- Root cause identification: Did you find the correct file(s) where the bug originates?
- Call chain accuracy: Did you trace the correct path from symptom to root cause?
- Fix quality: Is the proposed fix correct and minimal?

77-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed the comprehensive analysis of the Kafka producer buffer pool race condition. Let me create a summary of the key findings:

## Summary

I've identified and documented a **critical race condition** in the Apache Kafka producer's buffer pool management:

### The Bug
When in-flight `ProducerBatch` objects expire or when a broker disconnects, their pooled `ByteBuffer` objects are returned to the `BufferPool` and immediately reused for new batches—**while the original batch's request is still queued for serialization**. This causes data corruption where messages appear on the wrong topic.

### Root Cause Location
- **File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java`
- **Method**: `sendProducerData()` (line 357)
- **Critical Section**: Lines 395-442

### The Race Condition
1. **Line 395-396**: New batches are drained and added to in-flight tracking
2. **Line 406-418**: Expired batches are immediately deallocated, returning their buffers to the pool
3. **Line 442**: New produce requests are built and queued
4. **Line 874**: `batch.records()` creates a `MemoryRecords` object holding a **slice reference** to the pooled buffer
5. **Line 914**: `client.send()` queues the request but doesn't immediately serialize all data
6. **Problem**: By the time `client.poll()` actually sends the request to the network, the buffer may have been reused by another batch, corrupting the data

### The Fix
Move batch expiration/deallocation **after** `sendProduceRequests()` completes, ensuring all buffer slices are created and requests are queued before any buffers are returned to the pool for reuse.

The detailed analysis with code snippets and the proposed fix has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`.

}\\n356: \\n357:     private long sendProducerData(long now) {\\n358:         MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\\n359:         // get the list of partitions with \\n565:     /**\\n566:      * Handle a produce response\\n567:      */\\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\\n604:                                 .stream()\\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\\n609: \\n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\\n613:                     // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\\n614:                     TopicPartition tp = (!r.topicId().equals(Uuid.ZERO_UUID) && topicNames.containsKey(r.topicId())) ?\\n615:                             new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\\n616:                             new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\\n617: \\n618:        completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\\n624:                 }));\\n625: \\n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\\n630:                         .collect(\\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\\n633:                     if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\\n634:                         updatedPartitions.forEach(\\n635:                             part -> log.debug(\\\"For {} leader was updated.\\\", part)\\n636:                         );\\n637:                     }\\n638:                 }\\n639: \\n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\\n641:             } else {\\n642:                 // this is the acks = 0 case, just complete all requests\\n643:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values()) {\\n644:                     completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NONE), correlationId, now, null);\\n645:                 }\\n646:             }\\n647:         }\\n648:     }\\n649: \\n650:     /**\\n651:      * Complete or retry the given batch of records.\\n652:      *\\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\\n654:      * @param response The produce response\\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\\n658:      */\\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\\n662: \\n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\\n667:             log.warn(\\n668:                 \\\"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n669:                 correlationId,\\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\\n680:                 log.warn(\\n681:                     \\\"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n682:                     correlationId,\\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\\n691:                 //\\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\\n694:             } else {\\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\\n699:             }\\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\\n702:                     log.warn(\\\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \\\" +\\n703:                             \\\"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\\\",\\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\\n705:                 } else {\\n706:                     log.warn(\\\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \\\" +\\n707:                             \\\"to request metadata update now\\\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\\n708:                 }\\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\\n710:                     log.debug(\\\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\\\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\\n715:                     }\\n716:                 }\\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n718:             }\\n719:         } else {\\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\\n721:         }\\n722: \\n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\\n726:     }\\n727: \\n728:     /**\\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\\n730:      * e.g \\\"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\\\"\\n731:      */\\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\\n734:                 \\\"\\\" : String.format(\\\". Error Message: %s\\\", response.errorMessage);\\n735:         return String.format(\\\"%s%s\\\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\\n736:     }\\n737: \\n738:     private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\\n739:         this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\\n740:         maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\\n741:         this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n742:     }\\n743: \\n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\\n747:         }\\n748: \\n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n751:         }\\n752:     }\\n753: \\n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\\\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\\\");\\n762:         else\\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\\n764: \\n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n767:         } else {\\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\\n779:                 } else {\\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\\n781:                 }\\n782: \\n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\\n785:                 if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\\n786:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\\n787:                 } else {\\n788:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\\n789:                 }\\n790:             }\\n791: \\n792:             Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\\n795:                     return exception;\\n796:                 } else {\\n797:                     // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\\n798:                     // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\\n799:                     // return a generic exception.\\n800:                     return new KafkaException(\\\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \\\" +\\n801:                         \\\"which had one more more invalid records\\\");\\n802:                 }\\n803:             };\\n804: \\n805:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n806:         }\\n807:     }\\n808: \\n809:     private void failBatch(\\n810:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n811:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n812:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n813:     ) {\\n814:         failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n815:     }\\n816: \\n817:     private void failBatch(\\n818:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n819:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n820:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\\n821:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n822:     ) {\\n823:         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n824: \\n825:         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\\n826:             if (transactionManager != null) {\\n827:                 try {\\n828:                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\\n829:                     // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\\n830:                     transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n831:                 } catch (Exception e) {\\n832:                     log.debug(\\\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\\\", e);\\n833:                 }\\n834:             }\\n835:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n836:         }\\n837:     }\\n838: \\n839:     /**\\n840:      * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\\n841:      * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\\n842:      * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\\n843:      */\\n844:     private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\\n845:         return !batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now) &&\\n846:             batch.attempts() < this.retries &&\\n847:             !batch.isDone() &&\\n848:             (transactionManager == null ?\\n849:                     response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\\n850:                     transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\\n851:     }\\n852: \\n853:     /**\\n854:      * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\\n855:      */\\n856:     private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> collated, long now) {\\n857:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> entry : collated.entrySet())\\n858:             sendProduceRequest(now, entry.getKey(), acks, requestTimeoutMs, entry.getValue());\\n859:     }\\n860: \\n861:     /**\\n862:      * Create a produce request from the given record batches\\n863:      */\\n864:     private void sendProduceRequest(long now, int destination, short acks, int timeout, List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\\n865:         if (batches.isEmpty())\\n866:             return;\\n867: \\n868:         final Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> recordsByPartition = new HashMap<>(batches.size());\\n869:         Map<String, Uuid> topicIds = topicIdsForBatches(batches);\\n870: \\n871:         ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection tpd = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection();\\n872:         for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\\n873:             TopicPartition tp = batch.topicPartition;\\n874:             MemoryRecords records = batch.records();\\n875:             Uuid topicId = topicIds.get(tp.topic());\\n876:             ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData .setTopicId(topicId).setName(tp.topic());\\n881:                 tpd.add(tpData);\\n882:             }\\n883: \\n884:             tpData.partitionData().add(new batch);\\n888:         }\\n889: \\n890:         String transactionalId = null;\\n891:         boolean useTransactionV1Version = false;\\n892:         if (transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isTransactional()) {\\n893:             transactionalId = transactionManager.transactionalId();\\n894:             useTransactionV1Version = !transactionManager.isTransactionV2Enabled();\\n895:         }\\n896: \\n897:         ProduceRequest.Builder requestBuilder = ProduceRequest.builder(\\n898:                 new ProduceRequestData()\\n899:                         .setAcks(acks)\\n900:                         .setTimeoutMs(timeout)\\n901:                         .setTransactionalId(transactionalId)\\n902:                         .setTopicData(tpd),\\n903:                 useTransactionV1Version\\n904:         );\\n905:         // Fetch topic names from metadata outside callback as topic ids may change during the callback\\n906:         // for example if topic was recreated.\\n907:         Map<Uuid, String> topicNames = metadata.topicNames();\\n908: \\n909:         RequestCompletionHandler callback = response -> handleProduceResponse(response, recordsByPartition, topicNames, time.milliseconds());\\n910: \\n911:         String nodeId = Integer.toString(destination);\\n912:         ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(nodeId, requestBuilder, now, acks != 0,\\n913:                 requestTimeoutMs, callback);\\n914:         client.send(clientRequest, now);\\n915:         log.trace(\\\"Sent produce request to {}: {}\\\", nodeId, requestBuilder);\\n916:     }\\n917: \\n918:     private Map<String, Uuid> topicIdsForBatches(List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\\n919:         return batches.stream()\\n920:                 .collect(Collectors.toMap(\\n921:                         b -> b.topicPartition.topic(),\\n922:                         b -> metadata.topicIds().getOrDefault(b.topicPartition.topic(), Uuid.ZERO_UUID),\\n923:                         (existing, replacement) -> replacement)\\n924:                 );\\n925:     }\\n926: \\n927:   public void updateProduceRequestMetrics(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches) {\\n1037:             long now = time.milliseconds();\\n1038:             for (List<ProducerBatch> nodeBatch : transactionManager.authenticationFailed(e);\n335:             }\n336:         }\n337: \n338:         long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n339:         long pollTimeout = \n357:     private long sendProducerData(long now) {\n358:         MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\n359:         // get the list of partitions with data ready to send\n360:         RecordAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);\n361: \n362:         // if there are any partitions whose leaders are not known yet, force metadata update\n363:         if (!result.unknownLeaderTopics.isEmpty()) {\n364:             // The set of topics with unknown leader contains topics with leader election pending as well as\n365:             // topics which may have expired. Add the topic again to metadata to ensure it is included\n366:             // and request metadata update, since there are messages to send to the topic.\n367:             for (String topic :             if (!this.client.ready(node, now)) {\n381:                 // Update just the readyTimeMs of the latency stats, so that it moves forward\n382:                 // every time the batch is ready (then the difference between readyTimeMs and\n383:                 // drainTimeMs would represent how long data is waiting for the node).\n384:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, false);\n385:                 iter.remove();\n386:                 notReadyTimeout = Math.min(notReadyTimeout, this.client.pollDelayMs(node, now));\n387:             } else {\n388:                 // Update both readyTimeMs and drainTimeMs, this would \"reset\" the node\n389:                 // latency.\n390:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, true);\n391:             }\n392:         }\n393: \n394:         // create produce requests\n395:         Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> this.accumulator.mutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n402:             }\n403:         }\n404: \n405:         accumulator.resetNextBatchExpiryTime();\n406:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\n407:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\n408:         expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\n409: \n410:         // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\n411:         // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\n412:         // we need to reset the producer id here.\n413:         if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\n414:             log.trace(\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\", expiredBatches.size());\n415:         for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\n416:             String errorMessage = \"Expiring \" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \" record(s) for \" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\n417:                 + \":\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \" ms has passed since batch creation\";\n418:             failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\n419:             if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\n420:                 // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\n421:                 transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\n422:             }\n423:         }\n424:         sensors.updateProduceRequestMetrics(batches);\n425: \n426:         // If we have any nodes that are ready to send + have sendable data, poll with 0 timeout so this can immediately\n427:         // loop and try sending more data. Otherwise, the timeout will be the smaller value between next batch expiry\n428:         // time, and the delay time for checking data availability. Note that the nodes may have data that isn't yet\n429:         // sendable due to lingering, backing off, etc. This specifically does not include nodes with sendable data\n430:         // that aren't ready to send since they would cause busy looping.\n431:         long pollTimeout = Math.min(result.nextReadyCheckDelayMs, notReadyTimeout);\n432:         pollTimeout = Math.min(pollTimeout, this.accumulator.nextExpiryTimeMs() - now);\n433:         pollTimeout = Math.max(pollTimeout, 0);\n434:         if (!result.readyNodes.isEmpty()) {\n435:             log.trace(\"Nodes with data ready to send: {}\", result.readyNodes);\n436:             // if some partitions are already ready to be sent, the select time would be 0;\n437:             // otherwise if some partition already has some data accumulated but not ready yet,\n438:             // the select time will be the time difference between now and its linger expiry time;\n439:             // otherwise the select time will be the time difference between now and the metadata expiry time;\n440:             pollTimeout = 0;\n441:         }\n442:         sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\n443:         return pollTimeout;\n444:     }\n445: \n446:     /**\n447:      * Returns true if a transactional request is sent or polled, or if a FindCoordinator request is enqueued\n448:      */\n449:     private boolean maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest() {\n450:         if (transactionManager.hasInFlightRequest()) {\n451:             // as long as there are outstanding transactional requests, we simply wait for them to return\n452:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n453:             return true;\n454:         }\n455: \n456:         if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError()) accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(new TransactionAbortedException());\n460:         }\n461: \n462:         TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler = transactionManager.nextRequest(accumulator.hasIncomplete());\n463:         if (nextRequestHandler == null)\n464:             return false;\n465: \n466:         AbstractRequest.Builder<?> requestBuilder = nextRequestHandler.requestBuilder();\n467:         Node targetNode = null;\n468:         try {\n469:             FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType = nextRequestHandler.coordinatorType();\n470:             targetNode = coordinatorType != null ?\n471:                     transactionManager.coordinator(coordinatorType) :\n472: log.trace(\"Target node {} not ready within request timeout, will retry when node is ready.\", targetNode);\n476:                     maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n477:                     return true;\n478:                 }\n479:             } else if (coordinatorType != null) {\n480:                 log.trace(\"Coordinator not known for {}, will retry {} after finding               log.trace(\"No nodes available to send requests, will poll and retry when until a node is ready.\");\n485:                 transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n486:                 client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n487:                 return true;\n488:             }\n489: \n490:             if (nextRequestHandler.isRetry())\n491:                 time.sleep(nextRequestHandler.retryBackoffMs());\n492: \n493:             long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n494:             ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(targetNode.idString(), requestBuilder, currentTimeMs,\n495:                 true, requestTimeoutMs, nextRequestHandler);\n496:             log.debug(\"Sending transactional request {} to node {} with correlation ID {}\", requestBuilder, targetNode, clientRequest.correlationId());\n497:             client.send(clientRequest, currentTimeMs);\n498:             transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\n499:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n500:             return true;\n501:         } catch /**\n541:      * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\n542:      */\n543:     public void forceClose() {\n544:         this.forceClose = true;\n545: /**\n566:      * Handle a produce response\n567:      */\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\n569:         RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\n570:         int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\n571:         if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\n572:             log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\",\n573:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\n574:             for (ProducerBatch response, response.destination(), response.versionMismatch());\n586:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n587:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\n588:         } else {\n589:             log.trace(\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\", response.destination(), correlationId);\n590:             // if we have a response, parse it\n591:             if (response.hasResponse()) {\n592:                 // Sender should exercise PartitionProduceResponse rather than ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse\n593:                 // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\n594:                 ProduceResponse produceResponse partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\n597:                 produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\n600:              .stream()\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\n609: \n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\n613:                     // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\n614:                     TopicPartition tp =        new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\n617: \n618:                     ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\n619:                     if (batch == null) {\n620: + topicNames);\n622:                     }\n623:                     completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\n624:                 }));\n625: \n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\n630:                         .collect(\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\n633:                     if the given batch of records.\n652:      *\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\n654:      * @param response The produce response\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\n658:      */\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\n662: \n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\n667:             log.warn(\n668:                 \"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n669:                 correlationId,\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\n680:                 log.warn(\n681:                     \"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n682:                     correlationId,\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\n691:                 //\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\n694:             } else {\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\n699:             }\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\n702:                     log.warn(\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \" +\n703:                             \"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\",\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\n705:                 } else {\n706:                     log.warn(\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \" +\n707:                             \"to request metadata update now\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\n708:                 }\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\n710:                     log.debug(\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\n715:                     }\n716:                 }\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n718:             }\n719:         } else {\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\n721:         }\n722: \n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n726:     }\n727: \n728:     /**\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\n730:      * e.g \"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\"\n731:      */\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\n734:                 \"\" : String.format(\". this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n742:     }\n743: \n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\n747:         }\n748: \n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n751:         }\n752:     }\n753: \n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\");\n762:         else\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\n764: \n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n767:         } else {\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\n779:                 } else {\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\n781:                 }\n782: \n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\n785:                 if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\n786:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\n787:                 } else {\n788:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\n789:                 }\n790:             }\n791: \n792:             Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\n795:                     return exception;\n796:                 } else {\n797:                     // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\n798:                     // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\n799:                     // return a generic exception.\n800:                     return new KafkaException(\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \" +\n801:                         \"which had one more more invalid records\");\n802:                 }\n803:             };\n804: \n805:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n806:         }\n807:     }\n808: \n809:     private void failBatch(\n810:         ProducerBatch batch,\n811:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\n812:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\n813:     ) {\n814:         failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n815:     }\n816: \n817:     private void failBatch(\n818:         ProducerBatch batch,\n819:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\n820:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\n821:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\n822:     ) {\n823:         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n824: \n825:         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\n826:             if (transactionManager != null) {\n827:                 try {\n828:                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\n829:                     // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\n830:                     transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n831:                 } catch (Exception e) {\n832:                     log.debug(\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\", e);\n833:                 }\n834:             }\n835:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n836:         }\n837:     }\n838: \n839:     /**\n840:      * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\n841:      * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\n842:      * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\n843:      */\n844:     private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\n845:         return !batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now) &&\n846:             batch.attempts() < this.retries &&\n847:             !batch.isDone() &&\n848:             (transactionManager == null ?\n849:                     response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\n850:                     transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\n851:     }\n852: \n853:     /**\n854:      * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\n855:      */\n856:     private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> collated, long now) {\n857:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> entry : collated.entrySet())\n858:             sendProduceRequest(now, entry.getKey(), acks, requestTimeoutMs, entry.getValue());\n859:     }\n860: \n861:     /**\n862:      * Create a produce request from the given record batches\n863:      */\n864:     private void sendProduceRequest(long now, int destination, short acks, int timeout, List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\n865:         if (batches.isEmpty())\n866:             return;\n867: \n868:         final Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> recordsByPartition = new HashMap<>(batches.size());\n869:         Map<String, Uuid> topicIds = topicIdsForBatches(batches);\n870: \n871:         ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection tpd = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection();\n872:         for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\n873:             TopicPartition tp = batch.topicPartition;\n874:             MemoryRecords records = batch.records();\n875:             Uuid topicId = topicIds.get(tp.topic());\n876:             ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData tpData .setTopicId(topicId).setName(tp.topic());\n881:                 tpd.add(tpData);\n882:             }\n883: \n884:             tpData.partitionData().add(new batch);\n888:         }\n889: \n890:         String transactionalId = null;\n891:         boolean useTransactionV1Version = false;\n892:         if (transactionManager != null && !transactionManager.isTransactionV2Enabled();\n895:         }\n896: \n897:         ProduceRequest.Builder requestBuilder = ProduceRequest.builder(\n898:                 new ProduceRequestData()\n899:                         .setAcks(acks)\n900:                         .setTimeoutMs(timeout)\n901:                         .setTransactionalId(transactionalId)\n902:                         .setTopicData(tpd),\n903:                 useTransactionV1Version\n904:         );\n905:         // Fetch topic names from metadata outside callback as topic ids may change during the callback\n906:         // for example if topic was recreated.\n907:         Map<Uuid, String> topicNames = metadata.topicNames();\n908: \n909:         RequestCompletionHandler callback = response -> handleProduceResponse(response, recordsByPartition, topicNames, time.milliseconds());\n910: \n911:         String nodeId = Integer.toString(destination);\n912:         ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(nodeId, requestBuilder, now, acks != 0,\n913:                 requestTimeoutMs, callback);\n914:         client.send(clientRequest, now);\n915:         log.trace(\"Sent produce request to {}: {}\", nodeId, requestBuilder);\n916:     }\n917: \n918:     private Map<String, Uuid> topicIdsForBatches(List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\n919:         return batches.stream()\n920:                 .collect(Collectors.toMap(\n921:                         b -> b.topicPartition.topic(),\n922:                         b -> metadata.topicIds().getOrDefault(b.topicPartition.topic(), Uuid.ZERO_UUID),\n923:                         (existing, replacement) -> replacement)\n924:                 );\n925:     }\n926: \n927:     /**\n928:      * Wake up the selector associated with this Line 1032: Calls `free.deallocate(batch.buffer(), batch.initialCapacity())`\n   - Buffer is immediately available for reuse\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java`\n\n**Function**: `sendProducerData()` (line 357)\n\n**Lines**: 395-442 (the critical section)\n\n**Explanation**:\n\nThe race condition occurs due to a critical ordering issue in `sendProducerData()`:\n\n```java\n// Line 395: Drain ready batches\nMap<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = this.accumulator.drain(metadataSnapshot, result.readyNodes, this.maxRequestSize, now);\n\n// Line 396: Add them to in-flight tracking\naddToInflightBatches(batches);\n\n// Lines 406-408: Get expired in-flight batches from PREVIOUS iterations\nList<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\nList<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\nexpiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\n\n// Lines 415-423: DEALLOCATE expired batches immediately\nfor (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\n    failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\n    // ... failBatch() calls maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch()\n    // ... which calls accumulator.deallocate() (line 1032)\n    // ... which returns buffer to pool IMMEDIATELY\n}\n\n// Line 442: Queue produce requests for the newly drained batches\nsendProduceRequests(batches, now);\n// ... sendProduceRequest() calls batch.records() (line 874)\n// ... which creates MemoryRecords from buffer.slice() (MemoryRecordsBuilder.close():384)\n// ... then calls client.send() (line 914)\n// ... which serializes the request\n```\n\n### The Problem Timeline:\n\n1. **Iteration N-1**: Batch A is sent and added to `inFlightBatches`\n2. **Iteration N**:\n   - Line 395: New batches B, C, D are drained (created minutes/seconds ago, buffered, now ready)\n   - Line 396: New batches are added to `inFlightBatches`\n   - Line 406-408: Batch A (from iteration N-1) is found to be expired\n   - Line 418: `failBatch(A)` is called\n   - Line 835: `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(A)` is called\n   - Line 1032: Batch A's buffer is **returned to the pool and immediately available for reuse**\n   - Line 442: `sendProduceRequests()` is called for batches B, C, D\n   - Line 874: `batch.records()` is called, which calls `MemoryRecordsBuilder.build()`\n   - Line 381-384 in MemoryRecordsBuilder.close():\n     ```java\n     ByteBuffer buffer = buffer().duplicate();\n     buffer.flip();\n     buffer.position(initialPosition);\n     builtRecords = MemoryRecords.readableRecords(buffer.slice());\n     ```\n   - The `buffer.slice()` creates a view of the ByteBuffer from the pool\n   - Line 914: `client.send()` immediately serializes the request using `request.toSend(header)` (line 608 in NetworkClient)\n   - **IF** the batch's buffer was deallocated and reused between step 7 and step 10, AND the serialization reads from the buffer before it's been reused, the data might be correct. But...\n\n3. **The actual race**: The serialization might not fully write all bytes to the network immediately. Some data might be buffered in the Send object. When `client.poll()` is called later (line 340 in runOnce()), the Selector actually writes the data to the socket. By that time, if the buffer has been reused by another batch, the data written will be corrupted.\n\n### Why Topic Name Corruption Occurs:\n\nThe Produce request has this structure:\n- Header (including batch metadata)\n- Request data (including topic name and partition)\n- Record batch data (including individual records)\n\nThe topic name is written from the `ProduceRequestData` object, which holds a reference to the topic name separate from the MemoryRecords buffer. However, if the serialization process reads partial data from the buffer (due to buffering), and the buffer is reused, subsequent reads will get data from the new batch's buffer, potentially reading the wrong topic name from a different batch's data.\n\n## Proposed Fix\n\nThe fix is to ensure that buffers are NOT deallocated while requests are still queued and pending serialization. There are several approaches:\n\n### Option 1: Deallocate batches AFTER sending produce requests (Recommended)\n\nMove the expiration/deallocation AFTER the produce requests are sent, so any in-flight batches' buffers remain valid until after the requests are queued:\n\n```diff\n--- a/clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java\n+++ b/clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java\n@@ -404,18 +404,6 @@ public class Sender implements Runnable {\n         accumulator.resetNextBatchExpiryTime();\n         List<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\n         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\n-        expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\n-\n-        // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\n-        // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\n-        // we need to reset the producer id here.\n-        if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\n-            log.trace(\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\", expiredBatches.size());\n-        for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\n-            String errorMessage = \"Expiring \" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \" record(s) for \" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\n-                + \":\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \" ms has passed since batch creation\";\n-            failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\n-            if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\n-                // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\n-                transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\n-            }\n         }\n         sensors.updateProduceRequestMetrics(batches);\n@@ -438,6 +426,25 @@ public class Sender implements Runnable {\n                 pollTimeout = 0;\n         }\n         sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\n+\n+        // Expire batches AFTER sending produce requests to ensure their buffers remain valid\n+        // during request serialization\n+        expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\n+\n+        // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\n+        // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\n+        // we need to reset the producer id here.\n+        if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\n+            log.trace(\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\", expiredBatches.size());\n+        for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\n+            String errorMessage = \"Expiring \" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \" record(s) for \" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\n+                + \":\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \" ms has passed since batch creation\";\n+            failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\n+            if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\n+                // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\n+                transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\n+            }\n+        }\n         return pollTimeout;\n     }\n```\n\n### How the Fix Works:\n\n1. Expired batches are now failed and deallocated AFTER `sendProduceRequests()` completes\n2. This ensures that when `sendProduceRequests()` calls `batch.records()` and `client.send()`, all buffers are still valid\n3. When `client.poll()` is called later to actually serialize and send the requests, the buffers have already been deallocated, but the Send objects have already captured the serialized data\n4. Any expired batches' requests that were already queued in previous iterations will still use their deallocated buffers, but those requests are either:\n   - Already in-flight with responses pending (safe to deallocate)\n   - Or haven't been queued yet (in which case they won't be sent)\n\n## Analysis\n\nThe root cause is a **timing/ordering bug** where:\n\n1. Expired batches are deallocated immediately, returning their buffers to the pool\n2. These buffers are immediately available for reuse by new batches\n3. New batches' requests are built and serialized using buffers that might have just been reallocated\n4. The requests are queued but not fully written to the socket until `client.poll()` is called\n5. By the time the data is actually transmitted, the buffer might contain different data (from a reused buffer)\n\nThe fix ensures serialization happens BEFORE deallocation, preventing the buffer from being reused while any request serialization is still in progress or pending.\n\n### Why the Fix is Minimal and Safe:\n\n- **Minimal**: Only moves the expiration logic after the send, no new data structures or complex synchronization\n- **Safe**: Expired batches are still properly failed and their callbacks are invoked\n- **Correct**: The only difference is the ORDER - expiration happens after queueing requests instead of before\n- **No deadlock**: The code flow remains the same, no new locks are introduced\n- **Backward compatible**: External behavior is identical from the user's perspective\n",

# Kafka Producer Buffer Pool Race Condition Analysis

## Files Examined

- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/Sender.java` — examined for `sendProducerData()` and `failBatch()` methods to understand batch lifecycle
- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/ProducerBatch.java` — examined to understand batch buffer management and `records()` method
- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/internals/RecordAccumulator.java` — examined for `deallocate()` method to understand when buffers are returned to pool
- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/record/MemoryRecordsBuilder.java` — examined to understand buffer lifecycle and when MemoryRecords are created
- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/NetworkClient.java` — examined to understand when requests are serialized and sent

   - The poll() is where requests are actually serialized and sent to network

   - Iterates through drained batches and calls `sendProduceRequest()`

   - Line 914: Calls `client.send()` which serializes and queues the request

   - Calls `recordsBuilder.build()`
